***пилить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пилить.html>пили́ть</a> (2359)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пилить.html>пили́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pilítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to saw <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">cut with a saw</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отец.html>оте́ц</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:пилить.html>пи́лит</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:во.html>во</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:двор.html>дворе́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дрова.html>дрова́</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Otéc <b>pílit</b> vo dvoré drová.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">The father is sawing firewood in the courtyard.</span></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfectives:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:распилить.html>распили́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">raspilítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отпилить.html>отпили́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">otpilítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:попилить.html>попили́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">popilítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to nag, to chastise</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to appropriate (illegally, especially of public money, slang for the practice in which private contractors pay kickbacks to the various officials who award them projects)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пилить.html>пили́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:бюджет.html>бюдже́т</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pilítʹ</b> bjudžét</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to cut/"saw" the budget</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to walk, to drive (especially of long distances)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to screw, to have sex with</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пилить.html>пили́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pilítʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to saw</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пилка.html>пи́лка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pílka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пилка.html>пи́лки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пилка.html>пи́лки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пилка.html>пи́лок</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">пи́лочка</b>)

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пилот.html>пило́т</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pilót</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пилот.html>пило́та</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пилот.html>пило́ты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пилот.html>пило́тов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">aviation</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> pilot</li>

<li><span style="font-style: italic;background-color:CCFFFF;cursor:help;" title="переносное значение">перен.</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:иерархический.html>иерархи́ческое</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сообщество.html>соо́бщество</a> n class="example-fullblock example-absent-block"><ul>
</ul></li>


<li><span style="font-style: italic;background-color:CCFFFF;cursor:help;" title="<a href = vnd.unilang:экономический.html>экономи́ческое</a>">экон.</span> мошенническая организация, построенная по иерархическому принципу, в которой более высокие уровни получают доход за счет выплат с более низких уровней <span class="example-fullblock"><ul>
<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black">АО «МММ» и некоторые другие «инвестиционные фонды» начала 90-х были типичными <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;">пирамидами</span>. </span></li>
</ul></li>

</ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пиратский.html>пира́тский</a> (14808)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пират.html>пира́т</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pirát</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ский</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-skij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пиратский.html>пира́тский</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pirátskij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> pirate</li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пировать.html>пирова́ть</a> (15965)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пир.html>пир</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pir</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ова́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

***пирог.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пирога.html>пиро́г</a> (7890)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">пирогъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pirogŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*pirogъ</i>, probably from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*pirъ</i> + <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*-ogъ</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">pieróg</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">пиріг</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pyrih</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пирога.html>пиро́г</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">piróg</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пирога.html>пирога́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пирога.html>пироги́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пирог.html>пирого́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>pie; pirog</li></ol>

***писаный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:писаный.html>пи́саный</a> (18996)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:писать.html>писа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pisátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-аный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-anyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:писаный.html>пи́саный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">písanyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)пи́санее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)пи́саней</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> written down, fixed in writing
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:писаный.html>пи́саная</a></b> были́на</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>písanaja</b> bylína</i> ― <span class="e-translation">written-down bylina <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">type of East Slavic oral epic</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> handwritten</li>
<li>written in color, decorated</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> very beautiful, as if painted or decorated</li>
<li>painted</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>Short forms <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:писанный.html>пи́сан</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:писанный.html>пи́сана</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:писанный.html>пи́сано</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:писанный.html>пи́саны</a></span> theoretically exist, but are usually avoided, as they are the same as the short forms of the past passive participle of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:писать.html>писа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pisátʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to write</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
